<li>1848: <a href="/wiki/Revolutions_of_1848" title="Revolutions of 1848">Revolutions of 1848</a> and publication of <i><a href="/wiki/The_Communist_Manifesto" title="The Communist Manifesto">The Communist Manifesto</a></i>.</li>
<li>1852: Start of the <a href="/wiki/Crimean_War" title="Crimean War">Crimean War</a>, which ends in 1855 in a defeat for Russia.</li>
<li>1859: <a href="/wiki/Charles_Darwin" title="Charles Darwin">Charles Darwin</a> publishes <i>On the Origin of Species</i>.</li>
<li>1861: <a href="/wiki/Unification_of_Italy" title="Unification of Italy">Unification of Italy</a> after victories by <a href="/wiki/Giuseppe_Garibaldi" title="Giuseppe Garibaldi">Giuseppe Garibaldi</a>.</li>
<li>1866: First commercially successful <a href="/wiki/Transatlantic_telegraph_cable" title="Transatlantic telegraph cable">transatlantic telegraph cable</a> is completed.</li>
<li>1860s: Russia <a href="/wiki/Emancipation_reform_of_1861" title="Emancipation reform of 1861">emancipates its serfs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Karl_Marx" title="Karl Marx">Karl Marx</a> completes the first volume of <i><a href="/wiki/Das_Kapital" title="Das Kapital">Das Kapital</a></i>.</li>
<li>1870: <a href="/wiki/Franco-Prussian_War" title="Franco-Prussian War">Franco-Prussian War</a> and the fall of the <a href="/wiki/Second_French_Empire" title="Second French Empire">Second French Empire</a>.</li>
<li>1871: <a href="/wiki/Unification_of_Germany" title="Unification of Germany">Unification of Germany</a> under the direction of <a href="/wiki/Otto_von_Bismarck" title="Otto von Bismarck">Otto von Bismarck</a>.</li>
<li>1873: <a href="/wiki/Panic_of_1873" title="Panic of 1873">Panic of 1873</a> occurs. The <a href="/wiki/Long_Depression" title="Long Depression">Long Depression</a> begins.</li>
<li>1878: Re-establishment of <a href="/wiki/Principality_of_Bulgaria" title="Principality of Bulgaria">Bulgaria</a>, independence of <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Serbia" title="Kingdom of Serbia">Serbia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Principality_of_Montenegro" title="Principality of Montenegro">Montenegro</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Romania" title="Kingdom of Romania">Romania</a></li>
<li>1885: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Karl_Benz" title="Karl Benz">Karl Benz</a> invents <a href="/wiki/Benz_Patent-Motorwagen" title="Benz Patent-Motorwagen">Benz Patent-Motorwagen</a>, the world's first automobile.</li>
<li>1885: First permanent citywide <a href="/wiki/Tram" title="Tram">electrical tram</a> system in Europe (in <a href="/wiki/Sarajevo" title="Sarajevo">Sarajevo</a>).</li>
<li>1895: <a href="/wiki/Auguste_and_Louis_Lumi%C3%A8re" title="Auguste and Louis Lumière">Auguste and Louis Lumière</a> begin exhibitions of projected films before the paying public with their <a href="/wiki/Cinematograph" title="Cinematograph">cinematograph</a>, a portable camera, printer, and projector.</li>
<li>1902: <a href="/wiki/Guglielmo_Marconi" title="Guglielmo Marconi">Guglielmo Marconi</a> sends first transatlantic radio transmission.</li>
<li>1914: <a href="/wiki/Archduke_Franz_Ferdinand_of_Austria" title="Archduke Franz Ferdinand of Austria">Archduke Franz Ferdinand of Austria</a> <a href="/wiki/Assassination_of_Archduke_Franz_Ferdinand" title="Assassination of Archduke Franz Ferdinand">is assassinated</a>; <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">World War I</a> begins.</li>
<li>1917: <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Vladimir Lenin</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bolshevik" title="Bolshevik">Bolsheviks</a> seize power in the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Revolution" title="Russian Revolution">Russian Revolution</a>. The ensuing <a href="/wiki/Russian_Civil_War" title="Russian Civil War">Russian Civil War</a> lasts until 1922.</li>
<li>1918: World War I ends with the defeat of Germany and the Central Powers. Ten million soldiers killed; collapse of Russian, German, Austrian, and Ottoman empires.</li>
<li>1918: Collapse of the German Empire and monarchic system; founding of <a href="/wiki/Weimar_Republic" title="Weimar Republic">Weimar Republic</a>.</li>
<li>1918: Worldwide Spanish flu epidemic kills millions in Europe.</li>
<li>1918: Austro-Hungarian Empire dissolves.</li>
<li>1919: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Versailles_Treaty" title="Versailles Treaty">Versailles Treaty</a> strips Germany of its colonies, several provinces and its navy and air force; limits army; Allies occupy western areas; reparations ordered.</li>
<li>1920: <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a> begins operations; largely ineffective; defunct by 1939.</li>
<li>1921–22: Ireland divided; Irish Free State becomes independent and civil war erupts.</li>
<li>1922: <a href="/wiki/Benito_Mussolini" title="Benito Mussolini">Benito Mussolini</a> and the <a href="/wiki/National_Fascist_Party" title="National Fascist Party">Fascists</a> take power in Italy.</li>
<li>1929: Worldwide <a href="/wiki/Great_Depression" title="Great Depression">Great Depression</a> begins with <a href="/wiki/Wall_Street_Crash_of_1929" title="Wall Street Crash of 1929">stock market crash</a> in New York City.</li>
<li>1933: <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nazis" title="Nazis">Nazis</a> take power in Germany.</li>
<li>1935: Italy conquers Ethiopia; League sanctions are ineffective.</li>
<li>1936: Start of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Civil_War" title="Spanish Civil War">Spanish Civil War</a>; ends in 1939 with victory of Nationalists who are aided by Germany and Italy.</li>
<li>1938: Germany escalates the persecution of Jews with <a href="/wiki/Kristallnacht" title="Kristallnacht">Kristallnacht</a>.</li>
<li>1938: Appeasement of Germany by Britain and France; <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Munich_agreement" title="Munich agreement">Munich agreement</a> splits <a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">Czechoslovakia</a>; Germany seized the remainder in 1939.</li>
<li>1939: Britain and France hurriedly rearm; failed to arrange treaty with USSR.</li>
<li>1939: <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> and <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="Joseph Stalin">Joseph Stalin</a> agree partition of Eastern Europe in <a href="/wiki/Molotov%E2%80%93Ribbentrop_Pact" title="Molotov–Ribbentrop Pact">Molotov–Ribbentrop Pact</a>.</li>
<li>1939: <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi Germany</a> <a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Poland" title="Invasion of Poland">invades</a> <a href="/wiki/Second_Polish_Republic" title="Second Polish Republic">Poland</a>, starting the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Second_World_War" title="Second World War">Second World War</a>.</li>
<li>1940: Great Britain under <a href="/wiki/Winston_Churchill" title="Winston Churchill">Winston Churchill</a> becomes the last nation to hold out against the Nazis after winning the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Britain" title="Battle of Britain">Battle of Britain</a>.</li>
<li>1941: U.S. begins large-scale <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lend-lease" title="Lend-lease">lend-lease</a> aid to Britain, Free France, the USSR and other <a href="/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_II" title="Allies of World War II">Allies</a>; Canada also provides financial aid.</li>
<li>1941: Germany invades the Soviet Union in <a href="/wiki/Operation_Barbarossa" title="Operation Barbarossa">Operation Barbarossa</a>; fails to capture Moscow or Leningrad.</li>
<li>1942: <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">Nazi Germany</a> commence the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Holocaust" title="Holocaust">Holocaust</a> – a <a href="/wiki/Final_Solution" title="Final Solution">Final Solution</a>, with the murder of 6 million Jews.</li>
<li>1943: After <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Stalingrad" title="Battle of Stalingrad">Stalingrad</a> and <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Kursk" title="Battle of Kursk">Kursk</a>, Soviet forces begin recapturing Nazi-occupied territory in the East.</li>
<li>1944: U.S., British and Canadian armed forces <a href="/wiki/Normandy_landings" title="Normandy landings">invade Nazi-occupied France</a> at <a href="/wiki/Normandy" title="Normandy">Normandy</a>.</li>
<li>1945: <a href="/wiki/Death_of_Adolf_Hitler" title="Death of Adolf Hitler">Hitler commits suicide</a>, Mussolini is executed. World War II ends with Europe in ruins and Germany defeated.</li>
<li>1945: <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> formed.</li>
<li>1947: The <a href="/wiki/British_Empire" title="British Empire">British Empire</a> begins a process of voluntarily dismantling with the granting of independence to India and Pakistan.</li>
<li>1947: <a href="/wiki/Cold_War" title="Cold War">Cold War</a> begins as Europe is polarized East versus West.</li>
<li>1948–1951: U.S. provides large sums to rebuild Western Europe through the <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Plan" title="Marshall Plan">Marshall Plan</a>; stimulates large-scale modernization of European industries and reduction of trade restrictions.</li>
<li>1949: The <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> alliance is established.</li>
<li>1955: USSR creates a rival military coalition, the <a href="/wiki/Warsaw_Pact" title="Warsaw Pact">Warsaw Pact</a>.</li>
<li>1950: The <a href="/wiki/Schuman_Declaration" title="Schuman Declaration">Schuman Declaration</a> begins the process of <a href="/wiki/European_integration" title="European integration">European integration</a>.</li>
<li>1954: The <a href="/wiki/French_colonial_empire" title="French colonial empire">French Empire</a> begins to be dismantled; Withdraws from Vietnam.</li>
<li>1956: <a href="/wiki/Suez_Crisis" title="Suez Crisis">Suez Crisis</a> signals the end of the effective power of the British Empire.</li>
<li>1956: <a href="/wiki/Hungarian_Revolution_of_1956" title="Hungarian Revolution of 1956">Hungarian Uprising</a> defeated by Soviet military forces.</li>
<li>1957: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Treaties_of_Rome" title="Treaties of Rome">Treaties of Rome</a> establish the <a href="/wiki/European_Economic_Community" title="European Economic Community">European Economic Community</a> from 1958.</li>
<li>1962: The <a href="/wiki/Second_Vatican_Council" title="Second Vatican Council">Second Vatican Council</a> opens and begins a period of reform in the <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">Catholic Church</a></li>
<li>1968: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/May_1968_events_in_France" title="May 1968 events in France">May 1968 events in France</a> lead France to the brink of revolution.</li>
<li>1968: The <a href="/wiki/Prague_Spring" title="Prague Spring">Prague Spring</a> is defeated by <a href="/wiki/Warsaw_Pact_invasion_of_Czechoslovakia" title="Warsaw Pact invasion of Czechoslovakia">Warsaw Pact military forces</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Club_of_Rome" title="Club of Rome">Club of Rome</a> is founded.</li>
<li>1980: The <a href="/wiki/Solidarity_(Polish_trade_union)" title="Solidarity (Polish trade union)">Solidarność</a> movement under <a href="/wiki/Lech_Wa%C5%82%C4%99sa" title="Lech Wałęsa">Lech Wałęsa</a> begins open, overground opposition to the Communist rule in Poland.</li>
<li>1985: <a href="/wiki/Mikhail_Gorbachev" title="Mikhail Gorbachev">Mikhail Gorbachev</a> becomes leader of the Soviet Union and <a href="/wiki/Perestroika" title="Perestroika">begins reforms</a> which inadvertently leads to the fall of Communism and the Soviet Union.</li>
<li>1986: <a href="/wiki/Chernobyl_disaster" title="Chernobyl disaster">Chernobyl disaster</a> occurs, the worst nuclear disaster in history.</li>
<li>1989: <a href="/wiki/Revolutions_of_1989" title="Revolutions of 1989">Communism overthrown</a> in all the <a href="/wiki/Warsaw_Pact" title="Warsaw Pact">Warsaw Pact</a> countries except the Soviet Union. Fall of the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Wall" title="Berlin Wall">Berlin Wall</a> (opening of unrestrained border crossings between east and west, which effectively deprived the wall of any relevance).</li>
<li>1990: <a href="/wiki/German_reunification" title="German reunification">Reunification of Germany</a>.</li>
<li>1991: <a href="/wiki/Breakup_of_Yugoslavia" title="Breakup of Yugoslavia">Breakup of Yugoslavia</a> and the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/Yugoslav_Wars" title="Yugoslav Wars">Yugoslav Wars</a>.</li>
<li>1991: <a href="/wiki/Dissolution_of_the_Soviet_Union" title="Dissolution of the Soviet Union">Dissolution of the Soviet Union</a> and the creation of the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">Commonwealth of Independent States</a>.</li>
<li>1993: <a href="/wiki/Maastricht_Treaty" title="Maastricht Treaty">Maastricht Treaty</a> establishes the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>.</li>
<li>1997–99: End of European <a href="/wiki/Western_imperialism_in_Asia" title="Western imperialism in Asia">colonial empires in Asia</a> with the handover of <a href="/wiki/British_Hong_Kong" title="British Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_Macau" title="Portuguese Macau">Macau</a> to China.</li>
<li>2004: Slovenia, Hungary, the Czech Republic, Slovakia, Poland, Lithuania, Latvia, Estonia, Cyprus and Malta <a href="/wiki/2004_enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="2004 enlargement of the European Union">join the European Union</a>.</li>
<li>2007: Romania and Bulgaria <a href="/wiki/2007_enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="2007 enlargement of the European Union">join the European Union</a>.</li>
<li>2008: The <a href="/wiki/Great_Recession#Effects_on_Europe" title="Great Recession">Great Recession</a> begins. Unemployment rises in some parts of Europe.</li>
<li>2013: Croatia <a href="/wiki/2013_enlargement_of_the_European_Union" title="2013 enlargement of the European Union">joins</a> the European Union.</li>
<li>2014: <a href="/wiki/Revolution_of_Dignity" title="Revolution of Dignity">Revolution of Dignity</a> in Ukraine and the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_War" title="Russo-Ukrainian War">Russo-Ukrainian War</a>.</li>
<li>2015: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_migrant_crisis" title="European migrant crisis">European migrant crisis</a> starts.</li>
<li>2020: The United Kingdom <a href="/wiki/Brexit" title="Brexit">leaves the European Union</a>.</li>
<li>2020-ongoing: <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_Europe" title="COVID-19 pandemic in Europe">COVID-19 pandemic in Europe</a>, countries with the most cases are Russia, the United Kingdom, France, Spain, and Italy.</li>
<li>2022: <a href="/wiki/2022_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine" title="2022 Russian invasion of Ukraine">Russian invasion of Ukraine</a> opens with some of the most intense combat operations in Europe since the end of the Cold War.</li></ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=History_of_Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li id="cite_note-40"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-40">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090202191807/http://www.iht.com/articles/2008/01/04/arts/idbriefs5H.php" rel="nofollow">"The Great Arab Conquests"</a>. <i>International Herald Tribune</i>. 29 March 2009. Archived from <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/2008/01/04/arts/idbriefs5H.php" rel="nofollow">the original</a> on 2 February 2009<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">31 January</span> 2010</span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=International+Herald+Tribune&amp;rft.atitle=The+Great+Arab+Conquests&amp;rft.date=2009-03-29&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.iht.com%2Farticles%2F2008%2F01%2F04%2Farts%2Fidbriefs5H.php&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AHistory+of+Europe"></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-41"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-41">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="#CITEREFLaiouMorisson2007">Laiou &amp; Morisson 2007</a>, pp. 130–131; <a href="#CITEREFPounds1979">Pounds 1979</a>, p. 124.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-42"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-42">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Events used to mark the period's beginning include the sack of Rome by the <a href="/wiki/Goths" title="Goths">Goths</a> (410), the deposition of the last western <a href="/wiki/Roman_emperor" title="Roman emperor">Roman emperor</a> (476), the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Tolbiac" title="Battle of Tolbiac">Battle of Tolbiac</a> (496) and the <a href="/wiki/Gothic_War_(535%E2%80%93554)" title="Gothic War (535–554)">Gothic War</a> (535–552). Particular events taken to mark its end include the founding of the <a href="/wiki/Holy_Roman_Empire" title="Holy Roman Empire">Holy Roman Empire</a> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Otto_I_the_Great" title="Otto I the Great">Otto I the Great</a> (962), the <a href="/wiki/East%E2%80%93West_Schism" title="East–West Schism">Great Schism</a> (1054) and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Norman_conquest_of_England" title="Norman conquest of England">Norman conquest of England</a> (1066).</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-43"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-43">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFHunter2004">Hunter, Shireen;  et al. (2004). <i>Islam in Russia: The Politics of Identity and Security</i>. M.E. Sharpe. p. 3. <q>(..) It is difficult to establish exactly when Islam first appeared in Russia because the lands that Islam penetrated early in its expansion were not part of Russia at the time, but were later incorporated into the expanding Russian Empire. Islam reached the Caucasus region in the middle of the seventh century as part of the Arab <a href="/wiki/Muslim_conquest_of_Persia" title="Muslim conquest of Persia">conquest</a> of the Iranian Sassanian Empire.</q></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Islam+in+Russia%3A+The+Politics+of+Identity+and+Security&amp;rft.pages=3&amp;rft.pub=M.E.+Sharpe&amp;rft.date=2004&amp;rft.aulast=Hunter&amp;rft.aufirst=Shireen&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AHistory+of+Europe"></span></span>
</li>
